The court ordered both parties to complete the payment.

Adulterer Impersonates Detective 159

Trying to Take Away Paramour with Handcuffs

Exposed and Sent to Court Together

Huang Kejia, a farmer from Yuepu in the northeast of Wusong, reported to the local Security Corps on the morning of the day before yesterday that his nephew's wife, Huang Gu'shi, had eloped on September 26th of last year and had been missing ever since. He had recently learned that Gu'shi had secretly returned to Yuepu and was hiding in her mother's house. He requested her arrest. After receiving the report, the Security Corps immediately sent personnel to arrest Huang Gu'shi. She testified that she was 22 years old and that her husband, Huang A'fo, worked in a cigarette factory in Shanghai. She had married A'fo three years ago through a matchmaker. However, due to discord between the couple, they often quarreled. She ran away to Wusong in a fit of anger and worked in a textile factory. She then went to Shanghai and was introduced to work as a domestic helper. In Shanghai, she met Chen Xuedi from a certain advertising company, who seduced her into an affair that had occurred more than once. Recently, she fell in love with Chen and wanted to be with him permanently, so she returned to Yuepu to discuss a solution with her mother to sever her relationship with her husband. However, in the midst of the questioning, two young men in Western-style suits, carrying a pair of handcuffs, arrived at the Security Corps, claiming to be detectives from the Shanghai police and requesting to take Gu'shi back. The Security Corps suspected that they were suspicious and detained them, finding a badge. One of them confessed to being Gu'shi's lover, Chen Xuedi, and the other, Qiu Ding, was a patrolman in the Second District of Shanghai Special City. After reviewing the testimony, the Security Corps believed that Chen Xuedi, having taken another man's wife, dared to impersonate a detective to take her away, which was extremely illegal. They sent them all to the Public Security Bureau, sending a written report to the Baoshan County Public Security Bureau for strict investigation. They also ordered Huang A'fo, Gu'shi's husband, to come to the station for questioning.

Wang Lanying Meets an Unscrupulous Man 160

Huang Amao Utterly Destitute

Wang Lanying, a woman residing in the Laosanjing workshop in Pudong (and a party member), filed a lawsuit with the local court the other day, stating: "In the past, my parents arranged for me to marry Huang Amao, a Siyang native who worked as a matchmaker in Laosanjing, Pudong. It has been six or seven years now. However, Amao is addicted to opium and gambling, causing him to squander all the dowry I brought when I married. We have reached a point where we can't even afford to cook. My husband not only doesn't repent but also blames me for having bad luck and mistreats me. I had no choice but to work to support myself, which I have been doing for the past four years. The defendant not only doesn't show any compassion but constantly demands money from me. I am well aware of the principle of gender equality and therefore do not resent earning my own living. Recently, due to factory shutdowns, I have found it difficult to make a living, so I thought that my husband has a duty to support his wife. I returned home to seek a living, but to my surprise, there wasn't a grain of rice left in the house, and the defendant had pawned all my clothes. When I questioned him about it, I was severely beaten. I avoided him and returned after three days. Upon seeing me, the defendant still didn't let me go. Using rice as an excuse, he went out to a restaurant to fill his stomach. When I followed him, he dragged me back into the house and beat me again, causing further injuries. This is truly inhumane. I request an examination of my injuries and prosecution," etc. The prosecutor examined and confirmed that the injuries were real, ordered her to leave, and then immediately ordered the defendant to be summoned for investigation.

[P Reconciliation of Tang and Liu

Tang Senhe, a native of Taixian, Jiangbei, who lives on the Shanghai-Nanjing train line to make a living, resides in Datong Road, Zhabei. His wife, Ms. Liu, works in a silk factory and is quite beautiful. At the end of last year, she suddenly went missing. Shortly after, a man named Wang Zhaofu approached Tang to negotiate, saying that a certain Mr. Qin was willing to pay 120 yuan to take her abroad as her price, and begged Tang to give her up. Tang refused, leading to no results. Tang immediately filed a lawsuit with the local court, accusing Mr. Qin and Wang Zhaofu of colluding to hide his wife, etc. He was instructed to summon and detain Qin and others, and to await the arrest of Tang and Ms. Liu for questioning and verification. However, Tang and Ms. Liu stepped forward and hired a lawyer to file a personal lawsuit in the local court, requesting a divorce. On the tenth of this month, Judge Zhao Zhenhai held a hearing and repeatedly advised the plaintiff, Tang and Ms. Liu, to go out and reconcile. Meanwhile, Tang's father, Tang Shoushan, and mother, Tang Ying, dragged their daughter-in-law, Tang Liu, into the criminal division of the court. Prosecutor Liu Pingfan held a hearing and ordered the detained Wang Zhaofu and others to be interrogated. Tang Liu was handed back to her husband for custody, and Wang and others were released. It is reported that Tang has withdrawn the lawsuit from the criminal division, but the personal lawsuit has not been concluded. The other day, Judge Zhao held another hearing and ordered Tang Liu and Tang Senhe to appear in court. He asked, "Have you reconciled outside?" Tang Liu replied, "I have already returned home and am no longer pursuing the lawsuit. I was previously fooled by others and involved in a lawsuit with my husband. Now, I am grateful for my husband's understanding, and we have reconciled. At the last hearing, I was also given earnest advice by the presiding judge. I am not made of wood or stone, and I deeply regret my previous foolish actions. I am now willing to correct my past mistakes," etc. Tang Senhe stated, "My wife has now realized her mistake, and I will not pursue the past. I am still willing to reunite," etc. The judge then gave both parties some guidance and prepared a reconciliation record, ordering both parties to sign it. The court was then adjourned. Before the hearing, the two parties were whispering to each other in the waiting room, showing smiles from time to time, and were unusually intimate. When they left the court, they smiled at each other again. It can be seen that husband and wife are still husband and wife.

Du Jing Attempts Suicide by Jumping into the River but Fails 164

A Disappointed Boy Scout Instructor

Who is the "Old Gentleman" Mentioned in His Suicide Note?

Yesterday evening at 5:00 PM, the No. 5 ferry at the Chunjiang Wharf in Lujiazui, Pudong, was carrying passengers across the river. A passenger wearing a tattered Boy Scout uniform suddenly jumped into the river to commit suicide just a few feet away from the wharf. Fortunately, the water was shallow, and he was immediately rescued by the boatman and sent to the Water Police Station. He confessed that his name was Du Jing, 23 years old, from Guangdong. He used to be a Boy Scout instructor but is now unemployed. He felt that the environment was bad, so he attempted to commit suicide by jumping into the river. A copper badge was found on him, engraved with the words "Chinese Nationalist Party Boy Scout," and a suicide note. The envelope was addressed to Luo Jingshen Tang, side room of Mingfa Coal Store, Gonghe Lane, Dong Wuchang Road, Hongkou. The recipient was only addressed as "Old Gentleman" without specifying a name. The content roughly stated: "I cannot carry on the ancestral line and am deeply guilty. Even for one day, I cannot be allowed to remain in this world. I am oppressed by various environments and have no joy in life, so I have taken this drastic measure. However, who is without fault? To err is human, to forgive divine. I have realized this and am determined to correct my past mistakes and break the bad environment. But I am too guilty and cannot escape, leading to today's action." After reading it, the police chief asked who the "Old Gentleman" was. He replied that he was a relative but did not want to reveal his name, fearing that it would be published in the newspaper and affect his reputation. Since he had relatives in Shanghai, the police chief ordered detectives to investigate the address. However, there was no such person as "Old Gentleman" there, nor did anyone admit that Du Jing (the one who jumped into the river) was a relative. The detective returned to report. The police chief ordered the detective to send Du to Puxi and let him go home on his own.

The Dispute Between Uncle and Nephew Song 166

Song Luquan Detained for Three Days for Using Violence

Song Jinhui, from Yancheng, accompanied by his mother, Song Wang, twisted his uncle, Song Luquan, and his wife, Song Wang, to the Fourth District General Office to file a complaint. I make a living by pushing a cart, but business is not good. The income is not enough to maintain expenses, so I borrowed a few dollars from my uncle to avoid starvation. Unexpectedly, my uncle was not sympathetic and refused to give me a penny, pushing my mother and me out the door. My mother is already in her sixties. Unexpectedly, my uncle bullied me because I was poor and slapped my mother several times, and instigated his wife to beat my mother and me. My mother was injured in the waist and could not walk, so I twisted to the office to request an investigation. According to Song Wang's statement, it was roughly the same. According to Song Luquan's statement, the plaintiff's statement was completely untrue. My brother returned to his hometown a few days ago. I feel sorry for his poverty and provide him with food. Unexpectedly, my nephew is not satisfied. He insists that I make clothes for him. I think that my own economic situation is not very prosperous. I said that I would find a way after my brother came to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, he was dissatisfied and cursed at me. The Accounting Staff Embezzled the Workers' Salaries 174

The Family Tried to Raise the Money and Return It

A Three-Month Prison Sentence is Granted Probation

Qian Bochen, from Tongzhou, was introduced to the Huben Yarn Factory in Shanghai West as an apprentice. Because his service was considered diligent, he was promoted to the position of accounting staff last year. Unexpectedly, on December 14, Qian suddenly embezzled the huge sum of 1,967 yuan left over from the salaries paid to the workers in the yarn room of the factory and fled. After the board of directors of the factory learned about it, they reported it to the police station and requested an investigation. The other day, it was discovered that Qian was hiding in the Xinjilu Road in the city. Chinese and Western detectives rushed there and, together with the local Public Security Bureau, arrested Qian and took him to the Putuo Road Police Station for detention. His family was greatly panicked and immediately tried to raise about 1,300 yuan and return it to the factory. The remaining amount was to request the original recommender to take responsibility in order to reduce the crime. The next morning, the police station escorted Qian to the Provisional Court. The lawyer representing the factory appeared in court and explained the previous situation, requesting leniency. After Judge Luo interrogated the defendant, he was sentenced to three months in prison with leniency for being young and a first-time offender, and the embezzled money had already been returned, and he was given a two-year probation sentence in court.

Imprisonment for Two and a Half Years

Chen Yuhuai, from Fujian, rented a house at No. 362 Dagu Road and colluded with parties to privately manufacture counterfeit currency. A Fire in an Oil and Sesame Shop Was Extinguished Immediately 177

He Yuansheng's oil and sesame shop at No. 864 Limalu Road, Dongjiadu, Nanshi, has been open for more than 30 years and has a very good business. Around 5:00 AM yesterday, a fire suddenly broke out in the roof house behind the shop. In an instant, the flames soared and penetrated the roof. The fire brigade rang the alarm. Soon, fire brigades from various districts drove the pump trucks to the scene to connect water and extinguish the fire. After about half an hour, the smoke disappeared and the fire was extinguished. It was estimated that one roof house and two buildings of the shop were burned down, and the rest were not affected. When the fire was raging, Wang Xuemin, a guard at the 10th post of the police station, arrived and took Qin Fengbao, a partner of the shop, back to the first police station of the district in charge, and was ordered to stay temporarily for pre-trial investigation.

Wang Weigen was Detained for Selling Opium 178

At the back door of the South Railway Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, yesterday afternoon at 5:30 PM, a passenger, about 30 years old, purchased a ticket to Hangzhou. Gui Sheng, a policeman at the 32nd post of the Second District Police Station on Chezhan Road, saw that the passenger's appearance was suspicious, so he stepped forward to check. He copied 32 small bags and 15 large bags of opium, weighing more than 30 taels, from his side and detained the people and loot. After interrogation by Patrol Captain Ma, Wang Weigen, from Pudong, was immediately escorted to the Second District General Office and transferred to the court for trial.

[P Stealing Car Cushions, Each Detained for Five Days

Hu Yigui and Wang Dawangzi, both from Jiangbei, stole the seat cushions from the rickshaw pulled by Ma Arong in the French Concession the other day. Ma noticed it and the police arrested Hu and Wang and detained them in the police station. According to Hu's confession, he was instructed by Shen Xiaojiuzi to have people steal the cushions. The police chief ordered detectives to arrest Shen and bring him to justice. The plaintiff, Ma Arong, complained about the theft. When asked about Shen Xiaojiuzi's confession, he said that people have always pulled rickshaws to make a living. Because he was robbed of a seat cushion when he was pulling a rickshaw outside the other day, he could not afford to pay for it, so he asked his friends Hu Yigui and others to steal the cushions from Ma and return them to the rickshaw owner to avoid compensation. The judge sentenced the defendants to five days of detention each as a warning.

Art Circle

The Artification of Southern European Christianity 182

— Zhenxia

The morality of Christendom in Europe, though moderate and simple, is full of the superhuman doctrines of old Hebrew. However, when it comes to the Latin people of Southern Europe, who are as passionate as fire, with their wine and song, silk and steel, love and hate, their physical enjoyment, reckless and unyielding bravery, and the spirit of preferring sweetness first and bitterness later, preparing to roll into hell, are always impossible to soften, making it difficult for their souls to hope for heaven.

Southern Europe, near the Mediterranean, was the earliest place where the apostles preached the gospel. Logically, the development of Hebrew thought should naturally be more intense than in other places. But at the same time, we must also understand that the Mediterranean region is also the base and birthplace of Greek culture. When Christians gained power, although they relied on the power of the Roman Empire to completely destroy the surface of many Greek cultures, Greek thought had already penetrated deeply into people's hearts and could not be destroyed. Therefore, even if the Pope sits high in the Roman palace, and the citizens trample on the withered bones of ancient heroes and sing hymns of praise, the deep-rooted nature of Greek culture remains the same. Northern European Christian countries, such as Germany and the Netherlands, can be more practical in religious ceremonies. While there are old and new factions, the solidity of the foundation of Greek culture is also an important reason. Not only have the people of Southern Europe not been cooled down by Christianity, but they have also transformed the appearance of Catholicism into beautiful art. The (festivals) inherited by France, Italy, and Spain, the grand parades, and the city-wide carnivals, in the eyes of the ancient Hebrew judges, are truly more sinful than the golden calf worship at the foot of Mount Sinai.

The decadence and absurdity of the late Roman Empire naturally made the people tired of the reality of life, so the new atmosphere of Peter and Paul took the opportunity to enter and destroy the Roman Empire. However, this was only a temporary curiosity of mankind. How could a truly cultured country accommodate many people praying to the sky? So, in the end, magnificent temples had to be built, and artistic decorations had to be extremely elaborate.

In short, although the Hebrew spirit destroyed Rome, in the end, the Greek spirit of Rome still annihilated the Hebrew spirit.

The history of the struggle between the Greek and Hebrew ideas is certainly not so simple. However, in the end, the accomplishments of mankind in life are always indestructible barriers. Otherwise, art would have no way to exert its strengths when encountering religion.

Four Kinds of Tibetan Essentials, Volume One, Have Been Published 183

The China Inner Academy at No. 5 Park Road, Nanjing, has published the first volume of Tibetan Essentials. This publication takes essential Buddhist scriptures, collates them with Sanskrit and Tibetan versions, arranges the differences, and meticulously examines and determines the definitive edition. Furthermore, it provides summaries and subtle explanations, revealing reading methods, with a preface for each type, greatly opening the door of convenience, and is truly a valuable book for researchers. The volume contains twenty-five types, of which four have already been published, with the remainder to be published monthly. (1) *Upaya-prajna*, Tibetan Essentials Edition, printed in three volumes in imitation of the Song Dynasty edition. This book is the second section of the *Great Prajna Sutra*, the last twenty chapters, detailing the meaning of *upaya* as ultimate. Nagarjuna's Madhyamaka school is entirely based on this. Now it is published separately, with a summary and notes for easy reading.

(2) The Fifth Section of the *Great Prajna Sutra*, Tibetan Essentials Edition, printed in two volumes in imitation of the Song Dynasty edition. The *Great Prajna Sutra* has six hundred volumes, with the main meaning in the first five sections in five parts. This fifth section is a selection of the first three parts. Now it is specially published separately, with a summary and notes for easy reading. (3) *Sandhinirmochana Sutra*, Tibetan Essentials Edition, printed in one volume in imitation of the Song Dynasty edition. The correct path of Buddhism lies in the environment, practice, and result. This sutra discusses all three doors, with unparalleled simplicity. Now it is published, exploring the meaning of the sutra, with a summary at the beginning, and collating various Chinese and Tibetan translations, clarifying the difficult passages, making it feel more clear and easy to read. (4) *Mulamadhyamakakarika*, Tibetan Essentials Edition, printed in one volume in imitation of the Song Dynasty edition. This book was formerly the theory followed by the Madhyamaka school. Now it is published, adopting various Sanskrit and Tibetan commentaries, collating and revising over one hundred erroneous omissions, and summarizing the meanings of both Nagarjuna's and Asanga's Madhyamaka schools, with a special summary indicating the reading method. The writing is both coherent and organized, and the meaning is refined and insightful.

An appendix is provided below, outlining the editorial and collation methods of the Tibetan Essentials. The Great Canon of all dynasties has ten defects: 1. Lack of systematic organization, 2. Unsimplified apocryphal books, 3. Multiple translations of one book, 4. Difficult and obscure translations, 5. Translations distorting the original meaning, 6. Alteration and falsification of the original text, 7. Errors in the order of chapters, omissions, and misspellings, 8. Groundless speculation in writings, 9. Empty and sparse meaning in commentaries, 10. Tedious elaboration to fill in gaps. These are known as one disordered, two spurious, three repetitive, four obscure, five distorting, six falsifying, seven erroneous, eight speculative, nine empty, and ten verbose. With such a desolate path, how can one travel far? To show the thoroughfare to benefit scholars, this is why the Tibetan Essentials are being produced. An outline of the methods is as follows: 1. Based on the normative learning of the five Indias, creating a systematic compilation and arrangement, extracting the essence of the canon, classifying it according to type, first presenting the outline, then elaborating on the details, dividing it into six volumes, with the example of each volume being the same, from simple to complex, leading people to enlightenment, faith, understanding, practice, and upholding, so that they will not deviate, perhaps. 2. Different editions, different translations, and different texts, using one as the main, and selecting the best of the others, correcting errors and resolving doubts (examples are given below), striving to make the meaning clear and the writing smooth, so that the true face leaps out. 3. For different editions of texts, the Southern and Northern Song editions are the main ones. Errors and omissions in the Yuan and Ming dynasties and unauthorized revisions in the Korean canon are known by comparing Sanskrit and Tibetan texts. This edition does not lightly change anything without conclusive evidence, eliminating the careless and destructive errors of various editions. 4. Differing translations and texts are compared with old interpretations, selecting the best and combining commentaries. If they are the same, the more fluent text is taken. If they are different, the learning of both schools is preserved. As for those that are doubtful or erroneous, they are all deleted, not insisting on a fixed and complete text, as preserving antiquity. Four examples are briefly given to show its scope. Even the so-called finely engraved canon of today, such as the Japanese Taisho Canon, has hundreds of errors when its content is examined (examples are given below). This is because the learning is both high and profound, and the writing is also deep and refined. Westerners are not always able to interpret the meaning, and it is difficult for the Japanese to perform the writing. It is necessary to use the meticulous methods of Han and Qing scholars of classical studies in our country, and the refined and subtle thoughts of Song and Ming scholars exploring the truth, moistening it with eloquence, and regulating it with chapters and sentences, so that even though the mandarin orange tree is transplanted, its fruit does not change and the ultimate principle is clearly expressed. Today is not as good as the past, and versatile talents are rare and difficult to find. We are striving to meet the challenge, and with the support of many, the four kindnesses and three sufferings are forgotten, and we are resolutely doing it, regardless of our own crudeness.

The Story of World Literature (145) 184

— Written by John Macy, translated by Hu Zhongchi, USA

Chapter 38: French Prose in the 19th Century

The great critics of that era, friends or enemies of these Romantic writers and poets, but generally considered, and still considered, friends of the best in French literature, were Sainte-Beuve. His importance is largely limited to France. Criticism is a form of writing that does not directly address areas far from people's interests in literature. There are few critics who are internationally important. In fact, it can be said that critics have little reputation outside their own country. Sainte-Beuve influenced Matthew Arnold and other English critics, and probably all literary critics in Europe learned from him. His great achievement was to give the French, and the world, a clear interpretation of French literature. However, the world does not read criticism. Some of Sainte-Beuve's essays have been translated into English, but he remains a closed book to those who do not read French. For those who read French, he is not only an open book, but also the opener of the books of all French literature before him, and often of his contemporaries who were misjudged by him (such as Balzac). However, in general, he observed with the wise and direct light of criticism. After Sainte-Beuve, no literate Frenchman had an excuse for not understanding his country's literature, and any foreigner who groped for the best things in French literature would not have a better way than to follow Sainte-Beuve's guidance.

The rational and critical aspect of the French spirit is probably its most powerful aspect. Although France has literary and artistic giants in all forms, it is manifested in Ernest Renan and H.A. Taine. Renan is best known for his *Life of Jesus*, a skeptical and pious work. Like all books on religious issues, it became material for controversy. Christians did not like the book, and pagans used it in a way that Renan did not expect. Renan himself made the problem even more complicated by denying any interest in literature. In his own view, he was a seeker of truth who had no concern for style, a historian. However, literature retaliates with forgiveness, and in *Life of Jesus*, one sees a book that, whether or not it is analytically beautiful or (scientifically) historical, is undeniably a work of art. It is an explanation and adaptation of the New Testament, realistically depicted in rich colors. Realistic depiction, because most of the book was written by Renan in Syria, in the middle of that scene. He aspired to be a historian, critic, philosopher, and orientalist. He was a historical artist. People deceive themselves and write things that are better than they know, and literature, that mysterious and incomprehensible goddess, adopts them.

Like Renan, H.A. Taine regarded himself more as a scientific historian and logician than as a literary scholar. In the second half of the 19th century, the scientific spirit dominated all fields of thought. The word "(scientific)" and the ideas or methods it represented were somewhat overused. There was a science of all human activities, even erotic affairs. This movement was a reaction to the loose thinking of the Romantic era, and Taine was the leader of this movement in France. He believed that for any person of genius, whether a politician or a poet, if we know for sure his race, his era, his social affairs, and his dominating ability, we can explain him. Under this formula, criticism largely becomes a matter of biography and history. Later, critics who felt that this did not fully explain human genius raised objections to Taine's method. In fact, Taine himself was a poet beyond what he knew. In his essays, his aesthetic enthusiasm often transported him out of that declared principle. For English readers, his value is immeasurable, because his great work *History of English Literature* can never be completely replaced by subsequent research. And it is extremely illuminating to look at English literature from the perspective of a great Frenchman. The English translation is excellent.

Sadness is usually regarded as something unique to the Romantic temperament. However, in France, those who praised the joy of life were the Romanticists such as Hugo, George Sand, and Dumas, while those who were considered sad and world-weary were the rationalist realists. Taine viewed humanity with almost gloomy resignation, and the novelists Flaubert, Maupassant, and Zola, who followed Balzac, shared Taine's dark mood. This was not due to his influence, but because of the atmosphere of the time, partly because the war of 1870 was dark.

Gustave Flaubert, with cold contempt, and at the same time with the sharp clairvoyant wisdom that peered into human life, and with a view of life made mature by satire that did not make us laugh, made his books difficult to popularize widely even in his own country. However, for readers interested in the art of writing, Flaubert is the pinnacle of perfection. He worked for as long as a week on just one page, striving to find the right words. And the result was not decorative, exaggerated, or artificial, but precise, compliant, and the words were so natural that they seemed to have discovered themselves. His most famous novel is *Madame Bovary*, a description of a frail woman and her licentious love affair with ordinary people in a monotonous town. Such a description seems unmoved, but it is a very great novel, not only for its complete style, but also for its faithfulness to the characters. The story is made of non-heroic, even uninteresting material, but the ordinary becomes extraordinary, and the progress of the story is as inevitable as the tide. Although it is difficult to reproduce Flaubert's (appropriate words), the sense of progress and truth is not lost in translation (there is a complete English translation).

Publishing News 189

Publication of the New Zhong Code Complete Book. Zhang Yanxiang previously invented the New Zhong Code, which is edited according to the 1929 International Telegraph Regulations and approved by the Ministry of Communications and registered by the Ministry of Interior. It can save more than one-third of the telegraph fees. The translation is still in Chinese characters, completely without error. In order to avoid retranslation, the New Zhong Code Complete Book has been published. It was published yesterday. Chinese single characters are arranged in the order of the new telegraph code, with the number telegraph code noted above and the New Zhong Code noted below. The arrangement program follows scientific methods, and the lines are clear, making inspection extremely convenient. Compared with the popular clear and secret code telegraph books, it has been improved a lot. In addition to single characters, there are single codes for numbers up to 2,000. In addition, there are about 1,500 phrases, and one code can represent two or more characters. Ordinary and specialized terms are collected in detail. In addition, there is a difficult character search table containing about 1,000 characters, arranged according to the number of strokes, to avoid difficulty in selecting telegraphs. There is also a list of registered telegraph addresses of Shanghai commercial firms, totaling 1,500 companies, for the convenience of out-of-town reporting and inspection. The address and name of the recipient are only charged as one character, saving a lot of money. There are also more than 300 major domestic place names and 100 foreign place names, all replaced with single codes. Chemical element names and newly created characters are added to the supplement, and a Chinese-English comparison table is attached. The rhyme code for the date and the abbreviation table for province names are placed under the telegraph translation characters to save time. At the end are attached multiple code tables and index tables. Looking at the whole book, the system is rigorous, and the application is extremely convenient. In addition, the organizational law and compilation examples are published at the beginning of the book, so that people can become familiar with it in a short time and avoid mistakes. It is a practical book for the business community. The book is fourteen inches high and eight and a half inches wide, and is finely printed on a thick volume of Daolin paper. The price is one yuan per book, including domestic and foreign postage. Registration costs an additional six cents. The publisher is the New Zhong Engineering Company at No. 7 Ningbo Road, Jiangxi Road Intersection, Shanghai.

Home
